

Here I maintain a curated list of MW-related papers posted on ArXiv. I try to keep it updated daily. Besides that, you can find the list of Astro-ph papers discussed during the **<span style="color: #FF8C00;">Galaxy Dynamics Group</span>** meeting at UCLan [here](/jc/uclan/), and during the **<span style="color: #FF8C00;">Milky Way Brazilian Group</span>** meeting [here](/jc/mwbr/). Check [my Mendeley library](https://www.mendeley.com/library/community/astro-ph) for a larger collection.

* [Ripples of Stellar Enrichment (RoSE) -- simulating element production and mixing in the Milky Way star-by-star](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29242)

* [The GALAH survey and Gaia DR2: Linking ridges, arches and vertical waves in the kinematics of the Milky Way](https://arxiv.org/abs/1902.10113)
* [A Gaia-Enceladus Analog in the EAGLE Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/1908.07080)
* [Disentangling the Arcturus stream](https://arxiv.org/abs/1909.04949)
* [The Inside-out Growth of the Galactic Disk](https://arxiv.org/abs/1909.07118)
* [Dependence of Galactic Halo Kinematics on the Adopted Galactic Potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/1909.11250)
* [The Imprint of Spiral Arms on the Galactic Rotation Curve](https://arxiv.org/abs/1909.11158)
* [Chemodynamics of outer halo dwarf stars, including potential members of Gaia-Enceladus and Gaia-Sequoia](https://arxiv.org/abs/1909.11969)
* [Tracing Kinematic and Chemical Properties of Sagittarius Stream by K-Giants, M-Giants, and BHB stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/1909.12558)
* [Features of the Residual Velocity Ellipsoid of Hot Subdwarfs from the Gaia DR2 Catalog](https://arxiv.org/abs/1909.13076)
* [A MUSE study of the fast bar in the weakly-interacting galaxy NGC 4264](https://arxiv.org/abs/1909.13523)
* [Stellar chromospheric activity and age relation from open clusters in the LAMOST Survey](https://arxiv.org/abs/1909.13520)
* [The contribution from rotating massive stars to the enrichment in Sr and Ba of the Milky Way](https://arxiv.org/abs/1909.04378)
